Bomb is a traditional Bavarian Helles brewed with some of the best malts around
No adjunct. No surprises
Just quality ingredients from quality suppliers
☂ The Style
Bomb Lager expresses itself unapologetically
Our hope is that it inspires our drinkers to do the same
☂ The Principle

That’s what we believe in, and that’s what we’ll stick up for
We hope you enjoy. Always do so responsibly!
